26.1.2024 13:11  x
26.1.2024 13:12  ## {{{ imports\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nimport os\n\n## }}}\n## {{{ def process_syllable_file\n\n\ndef process_syllable_file(\n    file_path,\n):  # --> me da la listita de freccias de la sílaba input\n    # Read the txt file and handle 'nan' values\n    data = np.genfromtxt(\n        file_path, delimiter=",", missing_values="nan", filling_values=np.nan\n    )\n\n    # Extract frequency values and remove NaN values\n    frequency_values = data[:, 1]\n    frequency_values = frequency_values[~np.isnan(frequency_values)]\n\n    return frequency_values\n\n\n## }}}\n## {{{ def frequencies_individual( ): --> appendea todas las freccias del indiv a una lista. el arg es A o 23 etc\n\n\ndef frequencies_individual(individual):\n    base_path = "/home/ttdduu/lsd/tesis/datos/input/pitches"\n    individual_path = os.path.join(base_path, individual)\n    # Initialize a list to store all frequencies for the individual\n    all_frequencies = []\n\n    # Walk through each song directory\n    for song_dir in os.listdir(individual_path):\n        song_path = os.path.join(individual_path, song_dir)\n\n        # Process each txt file in the song directory\n        for txt_file in os.listdir(song_path):\n            if txt_file.endswith(".txt"):\n                txt_file_path = os.path.join(song_path, txt_file)\n\n                # Process the syllable file and update the list of frequencies\n                frequencies = process_syllable_file(txt_file_path)\n                all_frequencies.extend(frequencies)\n    return all_frequencies\n\n\n## }}}\n## {{{ def indiv_stats(individual_path):\n\n\ndef indiv_stats(individual_path):\n    all_frequencies = frequencies_individual(individual_path)\n\n    # Calculate mean, sd, min, and max for the individual\n    individual_stats = {\n        "mean": np.mean(all_frequencies),\n        "sd": np.std(all_frequencies),\n        "min": np.min(all_frequencies),\n        "max": np.max(all_frequencies),\n    }\n\n    return individual_stats\n\n\n## }}}\n## {{{ def cuantificar():\n\n\ndef cuantificar():\n    base_path = "/home/ttdduu/lsd/tesis/datos/input/pitches"\n\n    individuals = ["19", "23", "34", "A", "B", "1", "AC1", "AC2", "CH"]\n    # Create a dictionary to store individual statistics\n    all_stats = {}\n\n    # Process each individual\n    for individual in individuals:\n        individual_path = os.path.join(base_path, individual)\n        individual_stats = indiv_stats(individual_path)\n        all_stats[individual] = individual_stats\n\n    # Print the results\n    for individual, stats in all_stats.items():\n        print(f"Individual {individual} statistics:")\n        for key, value in stats.items():\n            print(f"  {key}: {value}")\n        print("\n")\n\n\n## }}}\n## {{{ def plot_histogram(individual_frequencies, individual_name):\n\n\ndef plot_histogram(individual_name):\n    individual_frequencies = frequencies_individual(f"{individual_name}")\n    plt.hist(\n        individual_frequencies, bins=50, color="blue", edgecolor="black", alpha=0.7\n    )\n    plt.xlim(700, plt.xlim()[1])\n    plt.title(f"Histogram of Frequencies for Individual {individual_name}")\n    plt.xlabel("Frequency")\n    plt.ylabel("Count")\n    plt.show()\n\n\n## }}}\n## {{{ def plot_violin_for_all_individuals():\n\n# [[/home/ttdduu/lsd/tesis/extra_files/la_tesis/figs/cuantificaciones/violin.png|violin]]\n\nimport seaborn as sns\nimport pandas as pd\n\n\ndef plot_violin_for_all_individuals():\n    individuals = ["19", "23", "34", "A", "B", "1", "AC1", "AC2", "CH"]\n\n    # Create a DataFrame for seaborn\n    data = {"Individual": [], "Frequency": []}\n\n    for individual in individuals:\n        frequencies = frequencies_individual(individual)\n        normalized_counts = np.histogram(frequencies, bins=50, density=True)[0]\n\n        data["Individual"].extend([individual] * len(frequencies))\n        data["Frequency"].extend(frequencies)\n\n    df = pd.DataFrame(data)\n\n    # Create a violin plot\n    plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))\n    sns.violinplot(x="Individual", y="Frequency", data=df)\n    plt.title("Violin Plot of Normalized Frequency Counts for Each Individual")\n    plt.xlabel("Individual")\n    plt.ylabel("Normalized Frequency Count")\n\n    plt.show()\n\n\nplot_violin_for_all_individuals()\n\n## }}}
